Urges California to Revise Proposed Autonomous Vehicle Regulations That Do Not Adequately Protect the Public</h3>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-summary\">        <div class=\"field-content\">NSPE submitted public comment to the California Department of Motor Vehicles urging revisions to proposed autonomous vehicle regulations in order to ensure public safety. </div>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-link-to\">        <div class=\"field-content\"><a Bill</h3>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-summary\">        <div class=\"field-content\">NSPE and the Nevada Society of Professional Engineers beat back legislation (A.B. 353) that would erode occupational licensure in the state.</div>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-link-to\">        <div class=\"field-content\"><a href=\"https://www.nspe.org/resources/issues-and-advocacy/latest-news/nspe-and-the-nevada-society-resist-inflammatory\">Learn more</a></div>  </div>  </div>\n  <div class=\"views-row views-row-3 views-field-field-summary\">        <div class=\"field-content\">Learn about the councils, committees, task forces, organizational activities, and other projects to which you can offer your expertise.</div>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-link-to\">        <div class=\"field-content\"><a href=\"https://www.nspe.org/membership/2017-18-call-volunteers\">Learn <h3 class=\"field-content\">NSPE, Maine Society Oppose Legislation Repealing Continuing Education Requirements</h3>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-summary\">        <div class=\"field-content\">NSPE and the Maine Society of Professional Engineers are opposing legislation that would eliminate continuing education requirements in the state.</div>  </div>  \n  <div class=\"views-field views-field-field-link-to\">        <div class=\"field-content\"><a
